Test pass/fail tracking lives in [tests.md](tests.md), not this backlog. Use this file for bugs / features / audit findings only.

## ✅ Fixed

| 978 | **[macOS distribution] Mac bundles must ship as a `ditto` zip — copying CI artifacts through Windows breaks them.** Owner (no Mac) asked to refresh the `TDP/Mac` OneDrive folder (stale 9 June). Downloading the mac-validate `mac-plugins-release` artifact and inspecting it revealed every inner Mach-O is `-rw-r--r--` — the GitHub artifact download path **strips the Unix executable bit, symlinks, and the arm64 ad-hoc code signature**. Copying those into `TDP/Mac` would ship **broken** bundles: the `.app` won't launch (no +x), and Apple Silicon refuses an arm64 slice whose signature was invalidated — a **likely contributor to testers' earlier "can't open"** (beyond Gatekeeper #99). Can't repair Unix perms/signatures from Windows. **Fix:** [mac-validate.yml](.github/workflows/mac-validate.yml) now packages the bundles on the Mac runner with `ditto -c -k --sequesterRsrc --keepParent` (preserves perms/symlinks/signature) into `mu-family-mac.zip`, uploaded as `mac-plugins-release`. **New distribution flow:** owner downloads the artifact, places `mu-family-mac.zip` in `TDP/Mac` **without extracting on Windows**; testers extract it **on their Mac** (Finder), install the bundles, `xattr -dr com.apple.quarantine`. Requires a re-dispatch of mac-validate to produce the zip (the current Windows-side TDP/Mac bundles can't be made correct without a Mac run).  **✅ PROVEN: mac-validate run 27304718168 fully green** (universal build, lipo arm64+x86_64, pluginval, auval, mu-Tant + mu-Clid renders all passed); mu-family-mac.zip built via ditto, **verified all 19 Mach-O binaries executable (0o755)**, and **delivered to OneDrive TDP/Mac** + READ-ME-FIRST.txt. | ✅ Fixed | 831 |
| 977 | **[deploy reliability] VST3 OneDrive deploy can silently fail on a stale/dehydrated destination bundle.** Owner reported the OneDrive tester files still dated 9 June. Investigation: most products redeployed fine at v1.0.831, but **two were stranded** — `mu-Toni.vst3` (the deploy's `cmake -E copy_directory` in [cmake/DeployRelease.cmake](cmake/DeployRelease.cmake) runs with `ERROR_QUIET` and only emits a `message(WARNING)` on failure; the stale OneDrive bundle — likely OneDrive cloud-dehydrated / a locked sub-file — couldn't be overwritten, so the copy failed into a buried warning and the 9-June bundle persisted), and `mu-link.exe` (mu-link has **no `increment_build_number` dependency** and doesn't read the build number, so with unchanged source it never relinks → its POST_BUILD deploy never refreshes; its date tracks the last actual mu-link code change, which is correct-but-confusing). **Resolved this session manually:** removed the stale OneDrive `mu-Toni.vst3` and force-copied the fresh local bundle; force-rebuilt mu-link (deleted the exe) → redeployed. **All OneDrive plugin files now today @ v1.0.831.** **Owner clarification → no code fix needed:** mu-toni is a not-yet-worked-on scaffold (its stale date is irrelevant), and mu-link is largely independent of mu-core so its date correctly tracks its OWN last source change, not the family version (no version-sync wanted). The dehydration/silent-copy failure only struck **because** those targets are inactive — actively-deployed products (mu-clid/tant/on) stay hydrated and copy fine — so the `DeployRelease.cmake` remove-then-copy hardening is **dropped as low-value** (and it carried partial-removal risk on a tester-locked bundle). Closed: the immediate staleness is fixed; no deploy-script change. | ✅ Fixed | 831 |
| 976 | **[tooling] mu-Tant headless `--render` → guaranteed-audio Mac smoke (no sample dependency).** The mac-validate render evidence (#975) initially used the mu-Clid A-suite, whose presets can expect samples not present on CI → silent clips. mu-Tant is a wavetable synth, so a headless render produces a content-independent oscillator drone. Added [mu-tant/Source/Plugin/RenderMode.{h,cpp}](mu-tant/Source/Plugin/RenderMode.cpp) (mirrors mu-clid's: `--render --out <wav> [--seconds/--samplerate/--blocksize]`), wired into [StandaloneApp.cpp](mu-tant/Source/Plugin/StandaloneApp.cpp) (initialise → parse/execute/quit) + [CMakeLists](mu-tant/CMakeLists.txt) (Standalone-only TU). **Key gotcha found:** mu-Tant is **silent on load by design** — the gater returns Silence when stopped (`gateModeFor: !playing → Silence`) and when playing an empty pattern; the raw drone only passes with the **gater bypassed**. So `execute()` sets `v0_gate_bypass=1` before rendering (matches the owner's "open mu-Tant, click bypass, it drones"). Also corrected the **stale [PluginProcessor.h](mu-tant/Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.h) comment** that claimed "stopped → gate held open (audition)" — it's the opposite. New [tests/expectations/mutant_drone.json](tests/expectations/mutant_drone.json) (rms_dbfs ≥ −60 over 0.5–3.5 s). [mac-validate.yml](.github/workflows/mac-validate.yml) now renders the mu-Tant drone as a **hard gate** (mu-Clid A-suite demoted to a best-effort bonus). **Verified locally on Windows:** clean build → render → analyse PASS (drone ≈ **−14 dBFS**). The CI step itself only runs on a Mac dispatch.  **✅ PROVEN: mac-validate run 27304718168 fully green** (universal build, lipo arm64+x86_64, pluginval, auval, mu-Tant + mu-Clid renders all passed); mu-family-mac.zip built via ditto, **verified all 19 Mach-O binaries executable (0o755)**, and **delivered to OneDrive TDP/Mac** + READ-ME-FIRST.txt. | ✅ Fixed | 831 |
| 975 | **[CI/tooling] On-demand macOS validation workflow — test Mac builds before testers, without a Mac, minimising cost.** Owner has no Mac and macOS GitHub runners bill at **10× the minute rate**, so the goal is a cheap, opt-in way to vet the Mac build + produce an evidence pack to analyse before sending to testers. **Done:** (1) new [.github/workflows/mac-validate.yml](.github/workflows/mac-validate.yml) — **`workflow_dispatch` only** (manual, runs only when fired). One macOS job: configure+build **universal Release** (VST3/CLAP/Standalone/AU, all products) → **`lipo` hard gate** (arm64+x86_64 present) → **pluginval** the VST3s (headless host harness: instantiate, audio at many SR/block, state save/restore, param fuzz — hard gate, `strictness` dispatch input) → **`auval`** the AUs (report-only) → **render the mu-Clid A-suite to WAVs + `analyse.py`** (report-only — real Mac-rendered audio to download & listen to) → upload two artifacts: `mac-validation-report` (lipo/pluginval/auval logs + rendered WAVs) and `mac-plugins-release` (the built universal bundles). (2) [run-listening-tests.py](tests/scripts/run-listening-tests.py) made **cross-platform** (finds the `.app` binary on macOS / bare exe on Linux, not just `*.exe`) so the render pipeline runs on the Mac runner. (3) **Trimmed macOS off the every-push [ci.yml](.github/workflows/ci.yml) matrix** (Linux+Windows remain the cheap net) — the universal `lipo` gate from #972 relocated into mac-validate.yml. **Tradeoff:** no per-push Mac *compile* coverage — dispatch mac-validate before a release / after Mac-affecting changes. Does NOT sign/notarize (#99) — testers still need `xattr` quarantine-strip. Both workflows YAML-lint clean; only provable on an actual dispatch (owner-gated, costs minutes). **Follow-up fix:** added `set -o pipefail` to the configure/build/pluginval/mu-Tant-render steps — without it a `cmd | tee log` pipeline returns *tee's* exit (always 0), so the "hard gates" (pluginval, the mu-Tant render→analyse) would have gone **green even on failure**; pipefail makes them actually gate. Also tee the configure+build output into `report/` so a build-stage failure lands in the downloadable artifact, not only the Actions console. **First real dispatch (run 27291697372) result:** universal build compiled (first-ever Mac compile ✓), `lipo` universal ✓, pluginval all VST3s ✓, auval ✓, mu-Tant render wrote the WAV ✓ — **only** the analyse step failed: `analyse.py` imports scipy but the step pip-installed only numpy → `ModuleNotFoundError`. Fixed → `pip install numpy scipy`. Verified by downloading the run artifact and analysing the **actual Mac-rendered WAV** locally: drone = **−14.06 dBFS PASS** (the Mac build genuinely makes sound; only the dep was missing). The run's `mac-plugins-release` (universal, pluginval+lipo-validated) is already shippable; re-dispatch gives a clean green.  **✅ PROVEN: mac-validate run 27304718168 fully green** (universal build, lipo arm64+x86_64, pluginval, auval, mu-Tant + mu-Clid renders all passed); mu-family-mac.zip built via ditto, **verified all 19 Mach-O binaries executable (0o755)**, and **delivered to OneDrive TDP/Mac** + READ-ME-FIRST.txt. | ✅ Fixed | 831 |
| 974 | **[Fixed, family-wide via mu-core] External (DAW) sidechain produced no ducking / dead GR — the buffer clear was wiping the sidechain input.** Tester confirmed on **mu-tant in both VST3 and CLAP** (Amount full, kick on the SC bus) — so not CLAP-specific and not the three originally-hypothesised causes (Amt=0 / pre-824 build / CLAP bus disabled). **Real root cause:** every product declares a stereo **Sidechain input** + stereo **Output** bus — equal channel counts, so JUCE maps **both to the same process-buffer channels [0,1]**. Each product's `processBlock` calls `buffer.clear()` at the top, then read the sidechain via `getBusBuffer(buffer,true,0)` — but the clear had already **zeroed the shared channels**, so `extScL` pointed at silence → never crossed the duck threshold → no GR. **Fix (one place):** mu-core `MixerEngine` now owns a private `extScCapture` buffer (sized in `prepare`) + `copyExternalSidechain()`; `ProcessorBase::captureSidechainAndClear(buffer)` copies the SC bus into it **before** clearing. Each product's `processBlock` now calls that single shared primitive as its first line (replacing the bare `buffer.clear()`), and the ~12-line per-product extraction block was **deleted** (it was duplicated in all four — a prior parity violation now removed). Internal channel-to-channel sidechain (e.g. mu-on Bass↔Kick) was unaffected (reads mixer channel bufs, not the host buffer). All four products Debug+Release clean; ships v1.0.828. **Tester-confirmed working in Bitwig** (mu-tant, v1.0.828). | ✅ Fixed | 828 |
| 973 | **[UI→Fixed] Mixer channel strips showed stale "inactive" dimming (only channel 1 bright) after a preset/host-state load changed the rhythm count.** Tester (Bitwig) loaded a 5-rhythm preset but the mixer dimmed channels 2–5 as if inactive, even though audio was flowing. Root cause: each strip's `active`/name/colour (the dim overlay in [MixerChannel::paint](mu-core/UI/MixerChannel.cpp)) was set **only** in `MixerOverlay::buildChannels()`, which runs at construction and on `refresh()` — and `refresh()` is gated behind `isMixerVisible()` ([PluginEditor.cpp](mu-clid/Source/Plugin/PluginEditor.cpp)). `loadFromAPVTS()` (which runs on `visibilityChanged` + preset reload) refreshed params/sidechain sources but never the active state, so a count change while the mixer was hidden left the dim overlays stale when it was next shown. Fix (mu-core, family-wide): `loadFromAPVTS` now re-syncs every strip's `setActive`/`setChannelName`/`setChannelColour` from the live `getNumChannels()` each call (added a `setChannelColour` setter to [MixerChannel](mu-core/UI/MixerChannel.h)); lightweight (no component recreation, unlike buildChannels). Benefits mu-clid/mu-tant/mu-on/mu-toni mixers. | ✅ Fixed | 827 |
| 972 | **[macOS] Universal (arm64 + x86_64) builds so Intel Macs can load the plugins.** Testers reported the Mac binaries won't open (Gatekeeper warning that won't bypass). Two causes: (a) unsigned/un-notarized — the Apple side of #99, worked around tester-side via `xattr -dr com.apple.quarantine`; (b) **this item** — no `CMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES` was set, so the build only targets the CI runner's native arch (`macos-latest` = Apple Silicon → **arm64-only**), and an Intel Mac can't run an arm64-only binary at all (no Gatekeeper trick helps). Fix: set `CMAKE_OSX_ARCHITECTURES "arm64;x86_64"` (guarded `if(APPLE AND NOT DEFINED …)` so a local dev build can still override to a single arch for speed) in the root [CMakeLists.txt](CMakeLists.txt) **before `project()`** so the arch is honoured during toolchain setup; applies family-wide (every product builds universal with no per-product change). The `lipo -archs` arm64+x86_64 hard gate now lives in [mac-validate.yml](.github/workflows/mac-validate.yml) (#975). Verifiable only on a macOS runner (no local Mac); Windows/Linux configure unchanged (APPLE-guarded). Does **not** fix Gatekeeper — signing/notarization (#99) is still separate; until then Intel + Apple-Silicon testers both still need the `xattr` quarantine-strip.  **✅ PROVEN** on mac-validate run 27304718168: every built bundle is universal x86_64 arm64 (lipo hard gate passed). | ✅ Fixed | 831 |
| 971 | **[pluginval→Fixed] mu-Clid Lite crashed (null deref) on host state restore.** pluginval (#970) immediately caught it: `mu-Clid Lite.vst3` segfaulted (`0xC0000005`) in the **"Plugin state"** test — i.e. the host save→restore cycle a DAW runs every time a project reloads. Root cause: [PresetIO::restoreRhythmSample](mu-clid/Source/Plugin/PresetIO.cpp) dereferences `proc_.voiceEngines[i]` unconditionally (`->clearSample()` / `->loadFile()`), but the **Lite** (MIDI-effect) build never creates the voice engines (`#if !MUCLID_LITE_BUILD voiceEngines[0]=…` in [PluginProcessor.cpp](mu-clid/Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.cpp)), so on restore (empty sample path → the `clearSample()` branch) it hit a null pointer. The sibling restore site `forceSyncRhythmFromAPVTS` was already null-guarded (`if (voiceEngines[ri])`); this one wasn't. Fix: early-return in `restoreRhythmSample` when `voiceEngines[i]` is null — Lite has no sample player to load into, and `loadedSamplePaths` is maintained by the caller. Full build unaffected (engine always non-null there). Verified: Lite VST3 now passes pluginval state test (5/5 family VST3s green). | ✅ Fixed | 825 |
| 970 | **[Tooling→Fixed] pluginval headless VST3 validation — Phase 1 shipped.** Added Tracktion's [pluginval](https://github.com/Tracktion/pluginval) to autonomously validate the family's built **VST3** binaries (mu-clid, mu-clid-lite, mu-tant, mu-toni, mu-on). pluginval hammers each plugin in a real host harness: instantiate, fuzz every parameter, run audio at many sample-rates/buffer-sizes, open/close editor, multiple instances, and **save→restore state and verify identity** — directly enforcing the "Everything in APVTS" cardinal rule (an un-persisted param fails restore) and the "audio thread never allocates / no NaN" rule (param-fuzz + denormal audio). **Coverage caveat:** pluginval validates VST3 + AU only — **not CLAP, not Standalone**; all formats wrap the same `ProcessorBase`, so VST3 covers the shared engine, but CLAP-*wrapper* bugs (cf. #969 CLAP sidechain) need a separate `clap-validator` pass (Phase 3). **Delivered:** (1) [tests/scripts/run-pluginval.ps1](tests/scripts/run-pluginval.ps1) — auto-downloads a pinned pluginval (or honours `$env:PLUGINVAL_PATH`), globs the per-product `build/<product>/<target>_artefacts/<Config>/VST3/*.vst3` bundles, runs `pluginval --strictness-level N --validate` per VST3, aggregates pass/fail, exits non-zero on any failure; flags `-Config Release` (default), `-Strictness`, `-SkipGui`; absent products (lite/toni in CI) are skipped not failed. (2) A Windows-only CI step in [.github/workflows/ci.yml](.github/workflows/ci.yml) running the script at strictness 5 as a hard gate. Caught #971 (Lite state-restore crash) on first run; after the fix **5/5 family VST3s pass at strictness 5**. **Follow-ups (Open, future):** Phase 2 — Linux (xvfb) + macOS (replace/complement `auval`), raise strictness toward 8–10; Phase 3 — `run-clapval.ps1` for CLAP-wrapper coverage. CI step proven only once pushed (no local green for the workflow itself). **CI fix (v1.0.830):** the first real CI run failed because JUCE leaves an **empty `.vst3` bundle skeleton** for an unbuilt target (CI builds a product subset), and pluginval failed that stub with "No types found"; the script now **skips any bundle with no compiled module inside** (checks for the inner `Contents/<arch>/<name>.vst3` file). Also added `mu-clid-lite_VST3` to the CI build so the shipping Lite variant is actually validated (not skipped) — it's the product that had #971. | ✅ Fixed | 825 |
| 969 | **[Fixed] CLAP sidechain input now exposed to hosts (was VST3-only).** The sidechain showed in **VST3** (via `SidechainVST3Extensions::getPluginHasMainInput()=false`) but NOT in **CLAP** (Bitwig) — the CLAP wrapper flags input port 0 as `CLAP_AUDIO_PORT_IS_MAIN` unless the processor implements `clap_juce_audio_processor_capabilities::isInputMain()`. Added the parallel CLAP capability in mu-core's [ProcessorBase](mu-core/Plugin/ProcessorBase.h) (one place → all four products): conditionally inherits `clap_juce_extensions::clap_juce_audio_processor_capabilities` and overrides `isInputMain(int)→false` so the lone input is a sidechain, not main. | 967 | **[Fixed] Stepped-mode modulator now tiles by step length too (follow-up to #963).** Extended the step-length tiling from Smooth to Stepped mode: [getStepCount](mu-core/Sequencer/ControlSequence.cpp) → `ceil(loop/step)` (with a 1e-9 guard so exact divisions don't round up) — 6 steps for Step 1/16×3 in a 1-bar loop (3,3,3,3,3,1), was `round`=5; [evaluateStepped](mu-core/Sequencer/ControlSequence.cpp) indexes by `phase / stepFraction` (tile by width) not `phase*count` (equal); [StepEditor](mu-core/UI/Components/StepEditor.cpp) gained `setStepFraction` and tiles its dividers/bars/hit-test at `k·stepFraction` with a narrower partial final cell; [ModulatorEditor::syncStepValues](mu-core/UI/ModulatorEditor.cpp) feeds it the fraction. Integer loop/step configs are byte-identical (ceil==round, `phase/frac`==`phase*count`); only non-integer (the broken case) changes. New tests: `getStepCount` 16/3→6 + an `evaluateStepped` per-cell read-back → mu-tant 132/132, mu-clid 140, mu-on 15. | ✅ Fixed | 821 |

| 965 | **[Fixed] Master VU + fader now come after the master insert effects.** Reordered the master stage in [MixerEngine::processBlock](mu-core/Audio/MixerEngine.cpp) from **fader → meter → inserts** to **inserts → fader → meter**: `masterInsert`/`masterInsert2` now process the summed bus first (pre-fader master-bus processing, so a master comp/limiter sees a consistent level), then `applyPanGain` applies the master level/pan, then `masterPeak` is captured — so the master VU reflects the true post-insert, post-fader output. | 963 | **[Fixed] Smooth-modulator step grid now tiles by the actual step length (partial final cell) instead of equal division.** Added [ControlSequence::getStepFraction()](mu-core/Sequencer/ControlSequence.cpp) (= `step/loop`, clamped to (0,1]); [LFOEditor](mu-core/UI/Components/LFOEditor.cpp) replaced its equal-`stepCount` grid + `snapX` with a `stepFraction` model — a grid line at each `k·stepFraction < 1`, so Step 1/16×3 in a 1-bar loop draws lines at 3/6/9/12/15 sixteenths = five 3/16 cells + a 1/16 remainder (was 5 equal cells from `round(16/3)=5`), and node X-snap lands on those real boundaries. | 962 | **[Fixed] Modulator smooth editor: double-click an existing node to delete it.** Added a `mouseDoubleClick` override to the shared [LFOEditor](mu-core/UI/Components/LFOEditor.cpp) that hit-tests the cursor and erases the node under it — same interior-only guard as right-click (the pinned x=0/x=1 boundary anchors are never deleted), resetting `dragIndex` so the trailing `mouseUp` (set by the second click's `mouseDown`) doesn't re-notify against shifted indices. | 961 | **[Audit→Fixed] HIGH** — ChorusEffect out-of-bounds read at high sample rates. [ChorusEffect.h](mu-core/Audio/FX/Send/ChorusEffect.h) no longer hard-codes a 4096-sample delay line: `prepareInner` now sizes each line to `jmax(4096, ceil(0.07·sr))` (covers the ~`0.06·sr` worst-case read offset + the Hermite +2 lookahead at any SR), `assign`s it (touches the pages — no first-touch fault), and the write-pos wrap uses the runtime `delaySize`. Above ~68 kHz the old fixed buffer made `hermiteDelay`'s `(writeP - offset + bufSize) % bufSize` go negative → heap over-read on the audio thread (UB/garbage/crash at 88.2/96/192 kHz); now the buffer always exceeds the max offset so the modulo stays in range. SendFXSmokeTests green (mu-clid 140, mu-tant 130). | ✅ Fixed | 815 |

Comment-only; the code was already correct. | ✅ Fixed | 815 |
| 957 | **[Fixed] Modulation curves clamped to the visible range — no more overshoot when bending or switching uni↔bipolar.** A bent segment's Catmull-Rom + `handleY` bezier control points, or a curve point's `y` after a polarity flip, could land outside the editor's 0..1 (unipolar) / -1..1 (bipolar) range, so the curve drew past the panel and the audio over/undershot the destination's swing. Fixes, all matched so drawing == audio: (1) [ControlSequence::evaluate](mu-core/Sequencer/ControlSequence.cpp) now clamps the output to the matrix contract (`0..100` / `-100..100`, not just the old unipolar floor); (2) [evaluateSmooth](mu-core/Sequencer/ControlSequence.cpp) + [LFOEditor::buildCurvePath](mu-core/UI/Components/LFOEditor.cpp) clamp the bezier control points `c1y`/`c2y` to the visible range (a bezier lies within its control hull → the segment can't overshoot); (3) anchors re-clamped on [LFOEditor::setUnipolar](mu-core/UI/Components/LFOEditor.h) + `setPoints`, and the stored `cs->curvePoints` re-clamped under lock on the polarity toggle in [ModulatorEditor](mu-core/UI/ModulatorEditor.cpp). 2-point/linear ramps unaffected (control points already in range) → all suites green (mu-clid 140, mu-tant 130, mu-on 15). Family-wide (every modulator + mu-on's Rumble bar envelope). | ✅ Fixed | 813 |
| 956 | **[Audit→Fixed] MED** — pinned mu-tant's `resolveLane` ordering coupling at **compile time**. Since `kTantModParams` + the `D_*` enum are file-local in [PluginProcessor.cpp](mu-tant/Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.cpp) (a runtime test can't see them), added a `constexpr` `static_assert` that `kTantModParams[i].destId == kModDestTable[i].id` for every `i` (plus representative `D_*`→dest pins), so any reorder/insert that would seed `resolveLane` with the wrong atom/range for a dest id now **fails to compile** instead of silently mis-routing modulation — stronger than the requested runtime test, and it can't be skipped. | 947 | **[Fixed] Drawable curve editor now bends smoothly through the points (no kinks).** The shared smooth-curve editor (`LFOEditor`) + its audio evaluator (`ControlSequence::evaluateSmooth`) interpolated each segment independently, so multi-point curves kinked at the anchors. | 945 | **[Fixed] mu-on: new "Rumble" lane — classic techno rumble framework.** Added a 5th lane ([MuOnChannels.h](mu-on/Source/Plugin/MuOnChannels.h): `Rumble=4`, `kNumChannels=5`, `kNumStepLanes=4`) that **processes the Kick's audio** rather than stepping. [RumbleEngine.h](mu-on/Source/Audio/RumbleEngine.h) runs the kick feed, in order, through: **(1)** input drive (the same MultiModeFilter valve), **(2)** three tempo-synced **delay taps** at 1/16·2/16·3/16, each with a level, **(3)** a **dark reverb** (mu-core `ReverbSlot` + a low-pass, with a **size** + dry/wet **mix** control, `r_revmix`), **(4)** a per-bar **volume envelope** — a **drawable smooth curve** (mu-core `LFOEditor`) that sits in the **step-grid slot** for the Rumble lane (the lane has no steps), persisted in state + evaluated audio-side under a try-lock, **(5)** a final multimode **filter**. The kick feed is stashed by [GrooveVoices](mu-on/Source/Audio/GrooveVoices.h) (Kick renders before Rumble) and fed in; the mixer strip gives Rumble a sidechain pre-wired to the Kick (amount 0 by default → optional kick-pumping). 9 engine params (`r_drive`/`r_d1..3`/`r_size`/`r_revmix`/`r_revlp`/`r_cut`/`r_res`) + per-lane mod dests ([MuOnModDest](mu-on/Source/Modulation/MuOnModDest.h), `.prop`); EnginePanel + sidebar + reset wired. **Framework status:** chain is audible end-to-end; the reverb tone + envelope curve-eval are basic and the per-block envelope is coarse (fine for now). | 934 | **[Fixed] Compiler warning C4244 in monocypher.c (u64→u32) — suppressed at build level, vendor source untouched.** The narrowing is on the whole RHS `lane * lane_size + (u32)ref` assigned to `u32 index` (not the explicit cast), in monocypher's Argon2 block-index math where the value is bounded well within u32. COMPILE_OPTIONS "/wd4244")` guarded by `if(MSVC)` in [mu-clid/CMakeLists.txt](mu-clid/CMakeLists.txt) (covers both mu-clid + mu-clid-lite, the two targets that compile it). | 933 | **[Fixed] Filter Drive onset made gradual (shared mu-core — mu-tant + mu-clid).** Reported the LP filter drive "kicks in instantly". Confirmed the drive path is identical shared code in both products — the saturation stage lives once in [MultiModeFilter::process](mu-core/Audio/MultiModeFilter.cpp#L74-L97): pre-gain → asymmetric soft-clip (`tanh` positive / `x/(1−x)` negative, for even harmonics) → `1/√preGain` makeup, bypassed at drive≈0. The harshness was the **linear** pre-gain ramp `1 + drv*5`, so low knob values already added a lot. Owner approved a gentler curve: changed the pre-gain to **squared** `1 + drv*drv*5`. Same endpoints (drv=0 → 1× clean, drv=1 → 6× full) so the max-drive ceiling and existing full-drive presets are unchanged, but the lower half of the knob is far gentler (drv=0.5 → 2.25× vs the old 3.5×; drv=0.2 → 1.2× vs 2×). Applies family-wide (it's the shared filter). NB the stage is still memoryless (not anti-aliased) — fine for warmth, can alias at extreme drive+input; oversampling is a separate future item if needed. mu-tant-tests 128/128; Debug clean across mu-tant + mu-clid. | ✅ Fixed | 795 |

| 929 | **mu-on: re-shaped the editor to the family per-voice layout (mirror mu-tant) — common interface; only the engine + step model differ.** ✅ Done at v1.0.794. mu-on's main panel ([GroovePanel.h](mu-on/Source/UI/GroovePanel.h)) is now the mu-tant `VoicePanel` shape, top→bottom: **(1)** shared `ChannelHeaderBar` (lane name + Reset — Reset clears the lane's engine params + modulators); **(2)** the selected lane's engine params ([EnginePanel](mu-on/Source/UI/EnginePanel.cpp)) directly under the header; **(3)** the 909 step editor shows **only the selected lane** — [GrooveGrid](mu-on/Source/UI/GrooveGrid.cpp) is now a single 16-step row (Swing/Accent stay in its knob strip), not the 4-row grid; **(4)** the shared mu-core `ModulatorPanel` at the bottom, identical to every other module. New per-lane modulation subsystem: `std::array<VoiceSlot,4> voiceSlots` on the processor, a per-lane [MuOnModDest](mu-on/Source/Modulation/MuOnModDest.h) provider (Kick/Bass/Hat/Snare each expose their own engine destinations), and [GrooveVoices](mu-on/Source/Audio/GrooveVoices.h) routes every engine param through that lane's `ModulationMatrix` each block (proportion-space seed → matrix → write-back; try-lock, zero-cost when unused). Engine params are seeded in 0..1 proportion and modulated via a **generic, plugin-agnostic** mu-core rule — destination ids ending `.prop` get `depthScaleFor` = 1.0 ([ModulationMatrix.cpp](mu-core/Modulation/ModulationMatrix.cpp)) — so a full-depth mod sweeps the whole knob (family "50% mod → 50% turn"). Per-lane modulators persist in a `<VoiceData>` child of the state tree (mirrors mu-tant); the ModulatorPanel rebinds slot + dest-provider on lane select and a 30 Hz timer drives its playhead. Boundary PASS (153 mu-core files); mu-on-tests 11/11 (added [ModulationTests.cpp](mu-on/Source/Tests/ModulationTests.cpp): `.prop` scale, lane-scoped dest tables, modulator round-trip dropping foreign-lane dests); Standalone + VST3 + CLAP Debug clean. **Follow-ups (still Open):** #926 (lift the EnginePanel knob-grid into a shared mu-core widget) is now framed as the next cleanup; `.muTrack` per-lane file I/O + Save-button wiring remain deferred with mu-on's preset chrome. | ✅ Fixed | 794 |

| 927 | **[Audit→Fixed] mu-on Bass filter envelope now opens on the onset block.** [BassEngine::render](mu-on/Source/Audio/BassEngine.h) computed the block-rate filter cutoff from the previous block's `t` (reset to 0 only inside the per-sample loop on `restart`), so the trigger block evaluated `fEnv≈0` and missed the filter-env "open" on the very attack it should brighten. | 924 | **[Audit→Fixed] mu-on sequencer onset is now sample-accurate end-to-end (offset is honored, not discarded).** The `GrooveSequencer` already computed a per-step `sampleOffset` (tested by the swing test) but the processBlock consumer ignored it and every engine restarted at sample 0. | 906 | **Compiler warning: MSVC C4996 'createWriterFor' deprecated overload — mis-attributed; real sites migrated to the modern API** Investigated the reported C4996 at `HarnessMain.cpp:132`. **The attribution was wrong on two counts:** (1) [HarnessMain.cpp:132](mu-link/Source/Tools/HarnessMain.cpp#L132) already uses the modern `createWriterFor(std::unique_ptr<OutputStream>&, AudioFormatWriterOptions)` overload (the lvalue `std::unique_ptr` binds the non-deprecated virtual; the deprecated `OutputStream*` overloads aren't even viable — a `unique_ptr` lvalue can't implicitly convert to a raw pointer), and a fresh `/W4 /diagnostics:column` recompile of `mu-link-harness` in **both** Debug and Release emits **0 warnings**. (2) The only genuine deprecated 6-arg `createWriterFor(OutputStream*, sr, ch, bits, {}, 0)` calls were elsewhere and already wrapped in `JUCE_BEGIN/END_IGNORE_WARNINGS_MSVC(4996)` (so they suppressed, not emitted, the warning) — in [tools/wavetable-gen/WavetableGen.cpp:145](tools/wavetable-gen/WavetableGen.cpp#L145) and [mu-tant/Source/Tests/SynthDSPTests.cpp:138](mu-tant/Source/Tests/SynthDSPTests.cpp#L138)+[:162](mu-tant/Source/Tests/SynthDSPTests.cpp#L162). **Fix (eliminate deprecated usage rather than hide it):** migrated all three real call sites to the modern `AudioFormatWriterOptions` overload (mirroring [RenderMode.cpp:259](mu-clid/Source/Plugin/RenderMode.cpp#L259)) — raw `new FileOutputStream`/`new MemoryOutputStream` + manual `delete` replaced with `std::unique_ptr<juce::OutputStream>` (writer takes ownership on success), and the three `JUCE_*_IGNORE_WARNINGS_MSVC(4996)` guards deleted. `mu-tant-wavetable-gen` + `mu-tant-tests` rebuild clean at `/W4`, 0 warnings; **mu-tant 127/127 green** (incl. the two migrated WAV-loader tests). | 904 | **mu-link Stage L7: external MIDI-clock sync (slave mode) — performance-critical** mu-link can now slave its master clock to incoming **MIDI clock**, selectable via a manual GUI toggle, without inheriting MIDI jitter — amends locked decision #4 (master-only) to master **or** external-MIDI-slave. **How it stays rock solid:** raw F8 pulses are never the timebase; new pure [MidiClockEstimator.h](mu-link/Source/Clock/MidiClockEstimator.h) is a **tempo PLL** — each F8 (24 ppqn) gives an instantaneous BPM from its interval, a one-pole filter (α=0.1, range-gated 20–400) smooths it, and only the transport *tempo* follows; the hardware frame counter remains the timebase, so clients + MIDI-clock-OUT stay sample-accurate. Handles FA/FB/FC (start/continue/stop) + Start→position-reset. [MidiClockInput.h](mu-link/Source/Clock/MidiClockInput.h) adapts a `juce::MidiInputCallback` to it (stamps pulses with monotonic hi-res time, not platform MIDI timestamps). `ServerEngine` gained `ClockSource` (Internal/ExternalMidi) — in external mode it pulls tempo/transport/reset from the estimator each block before publish/advance. `AudioServer` owns a `MidiClockInput`, registers it on the `AudioDeviceManager` for all enabled MIDI ins, exposes `setClockSource`/`externalBpm`/`externalRunning`. GUI: **Clock: Internal / Ext MIDI** toggle + MIDI-input options enabled in the device picker; external mode shows the detected BPM read-only on the tempo slider and locks the local tempo/play. Estimator unit-tested headless (converges 120→140 BPM, FA/FC transport edges) — **29/29 green**; mu-link-tests stays juce_core-only (the estimator is pure; the juce adapter lives only in AudioServer). | ✅ Fixed | 781 |
| 903 | **mu-link: master safety soft-clip on the bus sum (gain-staging audit)** Audited the full mu-clid→bus gain path after a "distorted crackling" report: the path is **unity end-to-end** (bridge `onRender` → `MuLinkClient` interleave → `ServerEngine` sum), per-client + master gain default 1.0 linear, so nothing inflates the level. Gap found: the master sum had **no clip protection** — a hot client (or the sum of several) could exceed ±1.0 and hard-clip the device. Added `masterSoftClip()` in `ServerEngine`: bit-exact below a 0.8 knee (~ -1.9 dBFS), C1-continuous into a `tanh` knee that asymptotes to ±1.0, applied after master gain. Normal-level material is untouched; the bus can never hard-clip regardless of client levels. Test added (hot 2.0 → ~1.0, normal 0.5 → 0.5 transparent); two existing tests rescaled to sub-knee levels (they used 100+/1.0 just to check the sum arithmetic). 28/28 green; `verify-bus.ps1` 3/3 (tones are below the knee, unaffected). NB: the *crackling* itself is most likely Debug-build under-runs (the producer can't sustain real-time) — being verified with a deploy-free Release build; the soft-clip addresses the *distortion* half. | ✅ Fixed | 780 |

| 901 | **mu-link Stage L6: per-client mixer + heartbeat reaping** **Mixer:** `ServerEngine` gained per-client **gain / pan (linear balance) / mute / solo** + **master gain** — atomics written by the message thread, read in `renderBlock`; a solo pass makes only soloed clients audible; post-fader peak feeds the meters. Implemented **directly in `ServerEngine`, NOT mu-core `MixerEngine`** (which is plugin-coupled — channels/FX sends); a lightweight server strip is the right tool and avoids dragging the plugin mixer into a server (documented deviation). Exposed via `AudioServer` setters and wired into the GUI: each client strip now has a gain knob + **M/S** toggles (mute red, solo amber), plus a master-gain knob under the master meter. **Heartbeat reaping:** `renderBlock` tracks per-slot frozen-heartbeat frames and reaps a slot (`active→0`) after >2 s of no heartbeat advance — a client that crashed without `detach()` no longer leaves a zombie slot/meter; `BlockStats::reapedClients` reports it. The GUI already polls `active`, so a reaped slot clears automatically. | 889 | **hot-swap: structural layer edits didn't cancel pending per-layer staged swaps (both products)** Found in the cross-product deep-dive audit. A per-layer hot-swap is staged by **index** in the stager; `addVoice`/`removeVoice`/`swapVoices`/`resetVoice` (mu-tant) and `addRhythm`/`removeRhythm`/`swapRhythms`/`resetRhythm` (mu-clid) shift/swap/clear slot data by index but never touched the stager — so a swap staged while playing, followed by a structural edit before the loop boundary, would commit to the **wrong slot** (a down-shift renumbers everything from the edit point; a swap transposes two slots; a removed index could go out of `numActive…` range and sit pending until a later grow re-commits stale data). Non-crashing (the install is a valid move) but wrong data. Fix: the structural-edit functions now cancel the affected pending per-layer swaps — `removeVoice`/`removeRhythm` cancel **all** (the renumber invalidates every higher index), `swap*` cancel the two slots, `reset*`/`add*` cancel the touched slot. A staged **full** preset is index-independent (replaces the whole state at commit) so it is left to win. mu-tant via `hotSwapStager.cancelVoice`, mu-clid via `hotSwapStager.cancelPendingIfAny`. 127 + 140 tests green. **NOTE:** mu-clid built + tested Debug only this session — needs a Release build to deploy the fix to testers. | ✅ Fixed | 776 |
| 888 | **mu-tant hot-swap: decode wavetables OFF the lock at stage time (kill the residual ~1-in-10 pause)** After #886 the *commit* was lock-free, but the *stage* (`preloadWavetablesFromState` → `bank.addOrLoadFile` under `voicesLock`) still did the whole WAV decode + FFT mip-build **inside** `voicesLock` — so loading a *new* preset every loop (stress test) decoded a new table under the lock at select time and the audio render bailed to silence for the decode duration ~1 in 10. Split `WavetableBank` into a lock-free decode + a locked append: new `decodeFile()` (file read + WAV decode + FFT mips → returns a `Wavetable`, no bank access) and `appendTable()` (the brief `push_back`); refactored `buildTable`→`buildTableData` (pure) + thin wrapper, `addFromWav`→`decodeWavData` (pure) + thin wrapper. `preloadWavetablesFromVoiceTree` now `findByPath`-skips already-loaded tables, **decodes off-lock**, and takes `voicesLock` only for the microsecond `appendTable`. **Readiness gate confirmed + documented:** the staging `isReady` store-release is set only AFTER the decode+append+parse complete, and `checkBoundaries` only commits `isReady` swaps — so if a loop boundary arrives before the new preset is ready, it is skipped and the swap commits at the next loop point (never a half-ready commit). 127 tests green. | ✅ Fixed | 775 |
| 887 | **docs: authoritative hot-swap reference** Deep-dived mu-clid's hot-swap (per-rhythm + full-preset) and documented it so future work can refer to it. | 886 | **mu-tant hot-swap: remove the last intermittent swap pause — resolve wavetables lock-free at commit** (follow-up to #885) After #885 the swap was seamless for index-based presets but still paused *intermittently* ("not every time") for presets whose oscillators select a table from the **Wavetables content folder** (selected **by path**, per #874). `readVoiceDataFromState` / `applyVoicePresetTree` resolved those paths at commit via `bank.addOrLoadFile()` **under `voicesLock`** — and any `voicesLock` hold, however brief, makes the audio render's `ScopedTryLock` bail to a full silent block for whatever block coincides (hence intermittent). Fix: at commit, resolve the bank index with the lock-free `WavetableBank::findByPath()` first (the hot-swap **stage** already pre-loaded every referenced table into the bank via `preloadWavetablesFromState`/`preloadWavetablesFromVoiceTree`), falling back to the locked `addOrLoadFile` disk load **only** when the table isn't already in the bank (stopped / immediate / host-restore paths, where the audio is silent or suspended anyway). The boundary commit now takes **no** `voicesLock` at all for a preloaded preset, so the render never bails → no pause. `findByPath` is a const read of the bank's table list; safe concurrent with the audio thread's by-index reads since no append happens during a commit (all appends are message-thread, serialised with the commit). 127 tests green. | ✅ Fixed | 774 |
| 885 | **mu-tant hot-swap: kill the swap-time transport freeze + silence gap, and wire the staging badges** (follow-up to #880/#883/#884) Two defects on a full-preset hot-swap while playing (factory tables): (1) **no staging badge** — the shared `TransportBar` "SWP" pill polls `ProcessorBase::hasPendingFullPreset()` and the shared `ChannelSidebar` polls `isPendingSwap(i)`, but mu-tant never overrode the former nor wired the latter, so neither badge showed. Added `PluginProcessor::hasPendingFullPreset()`→`hotSwapStager.hasFullPending()`, `hasPendingSwap(v)`/`cancelStagedSwap(v)`→ per-voice stager, and wired `VoiceSidebar.isPendingSwap`/`onCancelPendingSwap`. (2) **transport froze + audio went silent at the commit** — `applyFullPresetTree` ran the whole `replaceState` + `readVoiceDataFromState` + `syncAllFxParams` under a blanket `voicesLock`, so every `processBlock` bailed at its `tryLock` for the duration → multi-block silence AND a frozen `internalBeatPos` (the early-return also skipped the beat advance). Fix: (a) dropped the blanket lock from `applyFullPresetTree` — every structure it touches is already guarded by its own fine-grained lock the audio render respects (params atomic via `replaceState`; gates via `editLock` in `deserialiseGate`; modulators via `modLock` in `deserialise/clearModulators`; bank append self-locks), so the commit now runs concurrently with the render (a concurrent block sees old-or-new per structure, ≤1 block, inaudible) instead of silencing it; (b) restructured `processBlock` so the transport snapshot + beat advance + hot-swap boundary check run OUTSIDE the render `tryLock` (atomics only) → the transport never freezes even if the render momentarily bails. 127 tests green. | ✅ Fixed | 773 |
| 884 | **mu-tant: MIDI program-change preset loading (Ch 1-8 → voice slots, Ch 9 → full preset) + Settings page parity with mu-clid** Same model as mu-clid, reusing the mu-core `ProcessorBase` machinery (`scanMidiProgramChanges` / `drainPendingMidiProgramChanges` / `midiPresetMap` + `midiFullPresetMap`) and the shared `MidiPresetsPanel` / `MidiFullPresetsPanel` overlays. **Processor:** ctor points both maps at `<settingsDir>/muTant_midiPresets.json` + `muTant_midiFullPresets.json` and `.load()`s them; `processBlock` names the MidiBuffer + `if (scanMidiProgramChanges(midi)) triggerAsyncUpdate();` (before the voicesTryLock so PCs aren't dropped during a voice edit); `handleAsyncUpdate` calls `drainPendingMidiProgramChanges()`; the two apply hooks now route `applyMidiPresetSlot(slot,f) → loadVoicePreset(slot,f)` and `applyFullMidiPreset(f) → loadPreset(f)` (both hot-swap, so a PC defers to the loop boundary while playing). **Settings:** added a "MIDI Prog. | 883 | **mu-tant: per-voice (`.muPattern`) hot-swap — apply at THAT voice's own loop boundary** `loadVoicePreset` now parses to a ValueTree and, while playing, stages it in `VoiceHotSwapStager` (pre-loading referenced wavetables into the bank so the commit is disk-free), committing at the voice's **own** gate-pattern wrap (`gatePatterns[voice].patternLengthBars * 4`); while stopped it applies immediately. | 882 | **mu-core ModulatorEditor: Step selector left-justified next to the other controls, dice alone on the right** Follow-up to #873. | 881 | **mu-core filter: LP12 / all 12 dB SVF modes were very quiet — normalized resonance fed to the SVF as Q** The four SVF algorithms (`Lp12`/`Hp12`/`Bp12`/`Notch12`) passed the normalized `flt_res` (0..0.99, default 0.2) straight to `juce::dsp::StateVariableTPTFilter::setResonance`, which expects a **Q**. Q=0.2 is heavily over-damped (~-8 dB half an octave below cutoff, -14 dB at cutoff) → gutted passband, "very quiet"/dull; the Ladder modes correctly read 0..1 as resonance, so LP12 sounded quiet next to LP24. Added `mu_filter::svfResonanceToQ()` in `FilterAlgorithmBase.h` — maps res=0 → Q=0.707 (Butterworth, flat/full passband) rising exponentially to ~7.9 at res→1 — and routed all four SVF algorithms through it. Shared mu-core, so mu-clid's SVF filters get the same correction (a deliberate character change; the old behaviour was an over-damped bug). 120 tests green. | ✅ Fixed | 770 |
| 880 | **mu-tant: full-preset hot-swap — stage and switch at the loop boundary (product-side; mu-clid `HotSwapStager` NOT centralised to mu-core)** Implemented product-side per this session's decision (the mu-clid payload + boundary semantics are mu-clid-specific; only the ~30-line handshake is shared — a generic `mu-core BoundaryStager<Payload>` is deferred). `PluginProcessor` is now a `juce::AsyncUpdater`. `loadPreset` parses to a ValueTree and, while playing, pre-loads referenced wavetables + stages via `VoiceHotSwapStager::stageFull`, committing at **voice 0's** gate-pattern wrap; stopped → applies immediately. Boundary detection runs on the raw pre-ceiling beat position (`floor` loop-index crossing, so non-divisor lengths like 12/20 beats work) plus a playing→stopped edge (apply-on-stop). The immediate apply, the boundary commit, and host state-restore all share `applyFullPresetTree` (replaceState + numVoices + colours + readVoiceDataFromState + syncAllFxParams, under `voicesLock`). Commit fires `ProcessorBase::onPresetSwapCommitted` → editor re-runs `onPresetLoaded` (the shell's synchronous post-load refresh would otherwise paint stale state); editor clears both swap callbacks in its dtor (processor-outlives-editor UAF guard). Pure boundary predicates live in `Source/Plugin/HotSwapBoundary.h`; staging state machine in `Source/Plugin/VoiceHotSwapStager.h` — both header-only, unit-tested in `HotSwapBoundaryTests.cpp` (7 groups: wrap incl. non-divisors, stop-edge, full vs per-voice boundary, supersede, full-supersedes-voice). 127 tests green. | ✅ Fixed | 771 |
| 879 | **mu-tant: wavetable selection not restored in the dropdown after loading a preset (looked unsaved)** The data was always persisted correctly (verified on disk: `o1WtPath` on the `<Voice>` element + factory `o{1,2}_wt` in APVTS; `readVoiceDataFromState` re-resolves to a bank index so the engine/sound loaded the right table). Bug was UI-only: `refreshWavetableDropdowns()` ran only inside `rebindAttachments()`, which `setVoice()` skips when the voice index is unchanged — and preset load calls `onPresetLoaded → setVoice(0)` while already on voice 0, so the dropdowns never rebuilt and showed the stale selection. Fixed by calling `refreshWavetableDropdowns()` unconditionally in `setVoice()` alongside the other unconditional re-binds. | ✅ Fixed | 770 |
| 878 | **mu-link: new product — local audio receiver + master clock for the mu family (umbrella tracker — COMPLETE)** New sibling product. Role: present a low-latency audio sink that multiple mu standalone apps (mu-clid, mu-tant, future) output to, **sum** their streams, and render to one hardware device; **and** act as the family's rock-solid master clock so all products stay sample-accurately in sync. **Model (locked):** a **JACK-style local audio server with a shared-memory IPC bus** (NOT a system-wide virtual audio driver). mu-link owns the single hardware device (WASAPI/ASIO) and runs the one audio callback; clients push audio into per-client shared-memory ring buffers and read a shared **transport block** (sample position + tempo + play state) updated every callback — the hardware word clock IS the master clock (±0 drift), sidestepping MIDI-clock jitter. Click-avoidance via async double-buffered rings (underrun → silence, never glitches the master). Client side is a `mu-core` module (`MuLinkClient`) that swaps the JUCE output device for the bus and slaves `HostTransport`; falls back to its own device when mu-link isn't running. Outward bridge: real MIDI-clock OUT to outboard gear (no Ableton Link — avoids GPL). **STANDALONE-ONLY** — VST3/CLAP are never touched (host owns clock + audio I/O); every hook gated on `wrapperType_Standalone`; auto-detect via `OpenFileMapping`, self-register in the `ClientRegistry`, any launch order; reverts cleanly to its own device if mu-link quits mid-session. **All stages shipped:** **L1 ✅** (#893) Win32 shared-memory bus. **L2 ✅** (#895) `ServerEngine` + device-owning `AudioServer` + `mu-link-server`. **L3 ✅** (#897) GUI app (device picker, client/master meters, master transport). **L4 ✅** (#898) IPC contract + client glue lifted to `mu-core/Link/`. **L5 ✅** (#899) mu-clid standalone-only wired onto `MuLinkClient`. **L6 ✅** (#901) per-client gain/pan/mute/solo + master gain + GUI strips + heartbeat reaping; master soft-clip (#903). **L7 ✅** (#904) external MIDI-clock sync (slave mode) via a tempo PLL. **Shipped to testers at v1.0.782** (#905); **mu-Tant wired ✅** (#902) via the shared `mu-core/Link/MuLinkBridge.h` + `HostTransport` position standard. **CLOSED — manual hardware validation (tested OK at v1.0.793):** outboard MIDI sync confirmed against real gear, tested both ways — mu-clid slaved through mu-link (the bus carries clock + audio) **and** mu-clid standalone on its own (direct external-MIDI slave). The last umbrella residual (outboard MIDI-clock-OUT vs. real hardware) is cleared — mu-link is complete. | ✅ Fixed | 793 |
| 877 | **mu-tant wavetable: dropdown categories via sub-folders** (#874 follow-up 3) `VoicePanel::refreshWavetableDropdowns` ([VoicePanel.cpp:787](mu-tant/Source/UI/VoicePanel.cpp#L787)) now scans the `Wavetables` content folder **recursively** and groups files by their containing sub-folder: each sub-folder becomes its own `addSectionHeading` (nested paths shown `Parent / Child`), files in the root stay under "Wavetables". | 876 | **mu-tant wavetable: parse Serum `clm ` chunk for frame size** (#874 follow-up 2) `WavetableBank::addFromWav` previously hard-assumed `kFrameSize = 2048` samples/frame, mis-slicing Serum/Vital tables authored at other single-cycle lengths. Added a file-static `parseSerumFrameSize(data, numBytes)` ([WavetableBank.cpp](mu-tant/Source/Audio/WavetableBank.cpp)) that walks the RIFF chunk list for `clm ` and reads the integer after `<!>` (e.g. `"<!>1024 10000000 wavetable (...)"`). `addFromWav` uses the detected size when it's a power of two in `[kMinMipSize, 8192]` (FFT-order requirement), else falls back to `kFrameSize`; per-table `mipSize` already drives runtime sampling so non-2048 frames need no further change. New test splices a `clm ` chunk declaring 1024 into a 4096-sample WAV and asserts 4 frames (not 2). 120 tests green. | ✅ Fixed | 769 |
| 875 | **mu-core filter Drive: full unity-gain makeup collapses level past ~30% (thinned instead of fattening)** The pre-filter valve saturation in `MultiModeFilter::process` ([MultiModeFilter.cpp:82-95](mu-core/Audio/MultiModeFilter.cpp#L82-L95)) applied `preGain = 1 + drv·5` (1×..6×) then compensated with the **full inverse** `invGain = 1/preGain`. As drive rose, peaks clamped into the flat region of the tanh/algebraic curve while the makeup pulled the whole signal back down by the full gain — a 0.5-peak input dropped to ~0.34 at 30% drive and ~0.17 at 100%. Harmonics arrived but level collapsed → "lost body" rather than beefing up. Fix (option 1, loudness-neutral): makeup is now **`1/√preGain`** so quiet passages get boosted by the residual gain (adds thickness) and saturated peaks hold their level instead of being attenuated — same 0.5 input → ~0.41 at both 30% and 100%: level holds while harmonics build. One-line change in shared mu-core → mu-clid benefits too. The ×5 pre-gain ceiling and the asymmetric (tanh / x/(1−x)) curve are unchanged. | ✅ Fixed | 768 |
| 873 | **mu-core ModulatorEditor: step "× N" multiplier hidden behind the dice button** Follow-up to #872. Fix: in `ModulatorEditor::resized()`, place the dice first at `w - diceW`, then **right-anchor the step group** (label + note dropdown + "× N") immediately to the dice's left (`diceX - gap8 - nmW`, walking leftward), so the multiplier is always fully visible. The loop group still flows from the left; in Smooth mode (no step group) it never reaches the dice. | ✅ Fixed | 762 |

| 868 | **[Audit] MED — filter cutoff not clamped against Nyquist (SVF/Ladder instability at fs ≤ 40 kHz)** The 20 kHz APVTS cutoff ceiling exceeded Nyquist at sample rates ≤ 40 kHz; `StateVariableTPTFilter`/`LadderFilter` assert (debug) or destabilise (release) above fs/2. | 862 | **mu-tant/mu-core: Comb filter clicks under stepped cutoff modulation** A patch with Filter = Comb + a **Stepped** modulator on **Filter Cutoff** produced loud clicks on every step. Root cause in the **shared mu-core** `CombPlusFilter`/`CombMinusFilter`: the delay length (`delayF = sampleRate / cutoffHz`) was recomputed once per block from the **raw** cutoff and never smoothed, so a discrete cutoff jump moved the delay-line read tap discontinuously → a click. (Resonance was already smoothed; cutoff was not. Neither `VoiceEngine` (mu-clid) nor `SynthVoice` (mu-tant) slew-limits cutoff, so this affected **all** products that modulate a comb's cutoff — mu-clid only avoided it by not exercising that patch.) Fix: added a per-sample-smoothed `smoothedDelay` (`SmoothedValue`, 10 ms) to both comb filters; the ramp is pre-computed into a `delayRamp` scratch vector (sized at `prepare`) so every channel reads the identical glide (no L/R click). Stepped cutoff now glides the resonant pitch over 10 ms instead of clicking. Header-only change in mu-core → both products benefit. | ✅ Fixed | 756 |

| 844 | **Sidechain input bus declared as Vst::kMain instead of Vst::kAux — DAW never shows sidechain routing pin** Root cause: JUCE maps the first input bus to `Vst::kMain` by default unless `VST3ClientExtensions::getPluginHasMainInput()` returns false. For mu-family synths whose only input is a sidechain, `kMain` means Bitwig (and other DAWs) treat the bus as a main audio input rather than a routable sidechain pin. Fix: added `SidechainVST3Extensions` (overrides `getPluginHasMainInput() = false`) to `ProcessorBase`, and overrode `getVST3ClientExtensions()` on `ProcessorBase` to return it. All mu-family products now declare the sidechain as `Vst::kAux` automatically — new products inherit this for free without any product-level code. | ✅ Fixed | 740 |
| 843 | **mu-family Windows file properties: version, copyright, μ description** Root CMakeLists now reads `build_number.txt` at configure time (`MUFAMILY_BUILD_NUMBER`), computes `MUFAMILY_PLUGIN_VERSION = "1.0.N"` and `MUFAMILY_FILEVERSION = "1,0,N,0"` for VERSIONINFO, and `MUFAMILY_COPYRIGHT = "Copyright (c) YYYY Transwarp Development Project"`. All four `juce_add_plugin` calls (mu-tant, mu-clid, mu-clid-lite, mu-toni) set `VERSION` and `COMPANY_COPYRIGHT`. Custom `versioninfo.rc.in` templates (`configure_file` + `JUCE_USER_DEFINED_RC_FILE`) override JUCE's auto-generated VERSIONINFO so `FileDescription` / `ProductName` show `μ-Tant` / `μ-Clid` / `μ-Clid Lite` with the Greek mu. Templates live in each product's `resources/` folder. Version is configure-time accurate; reconfigure before each release session. | ✅ Fixed | 738 |

| 840 | **mu-tant transport regression guard: `HostTransport.h` + `PluginTransportTests`** Root-cause fix for the architectural gap that allowed #837 to ship. (1) New `mu-core/Plugin/HostTransport.h` — inline `mu_core::readHostTransport(AudioPlayHead*)` free function; all products call this instead of inlining their own `getPlayHead()` reads. (2) `mu-tant/Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.cpp` updated to use `readHostTransport` in the plugin-mode branch. (3) New `mu-tant/Source/Tests/PluginTransportTests.cpp` (6 tests) — `MockPlayHead` exercises `readHostTransport` with playing/stopped/no-BPM/no-position cases; two transport→gate contract tests assert gate silence when `readHostTransport` says stopped and gate audio when playing. All 118 mu-tant tests pass. | ✅ Fixed | 733 |
| 839 | **Root-cause analysis: how #837 was possible** `ProcessorBase::processCoreBlock` accepts pre-computed `effectiveBpm` and a render callback — it intentionally does not read the host playhead, delegating transport entirely to each product's `processBlock`. mu-clid has `deriveTransport`/`computeLiteTransport` that read `getPlayHead()`. mu-tant was written without this, leaving `playing` always `false` in plugin mode; `applyGateBlock(playing=false)` returns `GateMode::Silence` unconditionally. The existing unit tests could not catch this because they call `applyGateBlock` directly (no DAW context). Fixed architecturally by #840. | ✅ Fixed | 733 |
| 838 | **mu-tant X-MOD panel layout rearranged** Knob now centres horizontally above a single bottom row that groups Mode label + FM/AM/Ring/Off dropdown + Sync button side-by-side. | 837 | **mu-tant: no audio output in Bitwig (CLAP or VST3) — host transport not forwarded to the gate** Root cause: `processBlock` never read the host `AudioPlayHead`, so `blkPlaying` was always `false` in plugin mode (play button disabled + `playing` atomic initialised to `false`). `applyGateBlock` with `playing=false` outputs silence. Fix: added a `wrapperType != wrapperType_Standalone` branch in `processBlock` that reads `ph->getPosition()->getIsPlaying()` and `getBpm()` each block; stores host play state into the `playing` atomic (so `isInternalPlaying()` on the message thread reflects host state); uses host BPM for `blkBeatsPerSample`. Standalone path unchanged. | ✅ Fixed | 732 |

| 757 | **[family — delay→reverb intra-FX send broken in mu-tant/mu-toni (dly2rev not reaching engine)]** Moving the "Rev" send knob on the delay return strip in the mixer had no effect on the reverb level. | 756 | **[mu-tant — filter envelope slew-limited to match gate (eliminates clicks when envelopes out of sync)]** Filter envelope was being read directly without the 10 ms rise-limiting slew applied to the gate envelope, causing clicks when gate opened slowly but filter jumped instantly (e.g. filter 0→100 on attack while gate was ramping). Added `filterLevel` state field to `GatePattern` (analogous to `gateLevel`), applies same `maxRise` slew cap in `renderVoice` filter envelope block. Filter envelope now ramps at the same rate as gate on rising edge, preventing frequency-response artifacts when the two are out of sync. Backwards-compatible (no preset changes). | ✅ Fixed | 711 |

| 753 | **[mu-tant — filter envelope adds to base cutoff (was replacing it)]** Formula was multiplicative: `baseProp * (1 − depth*(1−fEnvVal))`, sweeping the filter from 0 Hz up to the base cutoff. Correct behaviour is additive: `clamp(baseProp + depth*fEnvVal)`, so envelope value 0 leaves the filter at its base cutoff and rising values open it above that point. Fixed in `PluginProcessor.cpp` `renderVoice` filter envelope block. | ✅ Fixed | 710 |

| 731 | **[build — tester-deploy kill-switch `MUFAMILY_DEPLOY_TESTERS` (default OFF)]** The OneDrive tester deploy (mu-clid main + Lite POST_BUILD steps) is now guarded by a root CMake option **defaulting OFF**, so no build pushes to the tester share — even an auto-backgrounded Release pass — unless explicitly opted in (`cmake -B build -DMUFAMILY_DEPLOY_TESTERS=ON`). **Why:** this environment auto-backgrounds long builds, and the background runner forces a `Debug && Release` pass, which fired the deploy repeatedly (v1.0.697–701) against the standing Debug-only/no-deploy policy — intent alone couldn't prevent it. | 727 | **[mu-tant — gater 0-attack de-click floor raised 3 → 10 ms (sustained low drone still clicked)]** The #726 rising-edge slew capped a 0-attack open at `kMinAttackMs` = **3 ms**, but on sustained low-frequency drone content a 3 ms linear ramp spans under ⅙ of a ~50 Hz cycle, so the amplitude step was still abrupt → audible tick (reported during live play-testing). Raised `GatePattern::kMinAttackMs` to **10 ms** ([GatePattern.h](mu-tant/Source/Sequencer/GatePattern.h)) — ~half a 50 Hz period, gradual enough to be click-free; mu-tant is a drone (no transients) so the longer floor costs nothing. Slew mechanism + falling/decay edges unchanged. `GateStageTests` "opens by end of block" now renders a block sized from `kMinAttackMs` (value-agnostic); CLAUDE.md + test comments updated off the stale 3 ms. 68/68 mu-tant; 140/140 mu-clid; boundary PASS. v1.0.699. | ✅ Fixed | 699 |
| 726 | **[mu-tant — gater rising-edge de-click: 0-attack envelopes ramp over ~kMinAttackMs]** A `split=0` (instant-attack) gate envelope opened the gate `0→1` in a single sample → audible click. `applyGateBlock` now slew-limits the **rising** edge of the gate signal to `GatePattern::kMinAttackMs` (~3 ms, [GatePattern.h](mu-tant/Source/Sequencer/GatePattern.h)): a 0-attack open ramps instead of jumping, while attacks drawn slower than the cap + all falling/decay edges pass through unchanged (drawn decay shapes preserved). Slew state (`GatePattern::gateLevel`) persists across blocks and resets when the gate is held closed; `applyGateBlock` gained a `sampleRate` arg and `renderVoice` passes `currentSampleRate`. `GateStageTests` updated (the "opens at start" assertion now expects the ramp) + a new test pins the ~3 ms ramp + per-sample slope cap. 65/65 mu-tant tests; standalone smoke OK. v1.0.696. **Note:** instant *closes* (a `split=1` region into silence, or a Gap edge) aren't slewed — add a release-side minimum if those click too. | ✅ Fixed | 696 |
| 725 | **[Audit→verified safe] FX algo change is already RT-allocation-free — no fix needed** The audit claimed `eff.setAlgorithm`/`rev.setAlgorithm` `make_unique`+`prepare` on the audio-thread `parameterChanged` path. Verified false: `EffectSlot::setAlgorithm` only flips an index into a **pre-allocated** algorithm array ([EffectSlot.cpp:42](mu-core/Audio/FX/Slots/EffectSlot.cpp#L42); ctor pre-allocs all algos, comment "never heap-allocates"); `ReverbSlot::setAlgorithm` allocates `impl` once in the ctor and hands params to the audio thread via a `PendingParams` snapshot ([ReverbSlot.cpp:129](mu-core/Audio/FX/Slots/ReverbSlot.cpp#L129)) — no inline alloc/prepare. Automating `eff_algo`/`rev_algo` does not allocate on the RT thread. Closed with no code change. v1.0.699. | ✅ Fixed | 699 |
| 724 | **[Audit→fixed] removed dead `eff_send` + `dly_send` (both inert, not just eff_send)** The audit premise was half-wrong: `dly_send` *was* wired (`dly.setSend`) but `DelaySlot::sendAmount` is **never read** by any audio path, and `eff_send` had no handler at all — both vestigial from a superseded send model (live sends are the channel `ch_sendEff/Dly/Rev` + inter-FX `eff2*/dly2rev`, all working). Removed `eff_send`/`dly_send` from `mu_mixfx::addGlobalFxParams` + mu-clid's layout + `kGlobalParamDefs` + sync handlers, and deleted `DelaySlot::setSend`/`sendAmount`. Surviving params' defaults/ranges unchanged; new mu-tant ApvtsLayout test (#721) guards their absence. 140/140 mu-clid + 68/68 mu-tant; boundary PASS. v1.0.699. | ✅ Fixed | 699 |

| 705 | **[mu-tant — internalBpm made atomic (audio-thread data race fixed)]** `internalBpm` was a plain `double` written by `setInternalBpm` (message thread, BPM box) and read every block by `processBlock` for `beatsPerSample` + passed as `effectiveBpm` — a non-atomic concurrent read/write (UB; a torn double / beat-advance glitch when changing tempo during playback). | 696 | **[mu-family — parity principle documented + mu-tant dynamic voice model (Stage 1 of the parity lift)]** Locked the family-parity working agreement: every mu-product shares ONE UX/GUI (shell, sidebar/layers, presets, panel styling, filter/insert/mixer, modulators) and only the **synth engine** differs; signal flow is `engine → insert → mixer`; all common code is centralised in mu-core (no duplication); mu-clid is the reference and every design choice gets documented. | 695 | **[mu-tant — gate off on load + audio test harness, single-voice default, full presets, mixer height]** Tester pass 3. **(1) Drone audible on load — fixed.** Reworked the gater: extracted the block-level decision into the shared `gateModeFor()` + `applyGateBlock()` ([GatePattern.{h,cpp}](mu-tant/Source/Sequencer/GatePattern.h)) — **bypassed → raw drone passes** (audition); **stopped → silent**; **playing + no envelopes → silent**; **playing + envelopes → per-sample envelope gate**. | 692 | **[mu-tant — drawable attack/decay gate editor + grab-handles + glue + Gap dial]** Reworked the gate model from the decay-only sketch into the interactive editor the design now specifies. **Model** ([GatePattern.{h,cpp}](mu-tant/Source/Sequencer/GatePattern.h)): `GateEnvelope` is now `startCell` + `lengthCells` + `split` (attack/decay peak position) + independent `attackBend` / `decayBend` (−1..+1, `pow(x, 2^(−bend·2))`) + `reverse` (mirror in time, swapping attack/decay). `value(phase01, gap01)` is the single shared evaluator: shape squeezed into the leading `(1−gap)` of the region, trailing `gap` forced silent. Envelopes are non-overlapping spans; `addEnvelope` trims overlaps, `removeEnvelopeCovering` removes by any interior cell, `mergeRange` glues a dragged span into one region averaging the merged shapes. `gateAt(beat, gap)` evaluates region-wide phase (not per-cell) with the cell→envelope cache. **Editor** ([GatingDesigner.{h,cpp}](mu-tant/Source/UI/GatingDesigner.h)): Pencil draws a 1-cell envelope and drags three grab-handles — top point = split, attack/decay line mid-grabs = bend — with the cursor turning to a hand on hover/drag; Eraser removes; Glue drag-merges (range highlight while dragging); Reverse flips a clicked envelope. Handles + curves render the exact gate the engine outputs (incl. the Gap silence tail). **Gap dial**: new per-voice APVTS param `v{N}_gate_gap` (0..1, shown 0–100%) + a Gap [KnobWithLabel](mu-core/UI/Components/KnobWithLabel.h) in the gating band ([VoicePanel](mu-tant/Source/UI/VoicePanel.h), rebound per voice, pushes its value into the designer for rendering); `processBlock` reads it into `gateAt`. Per-envelope probability / loop-N-of-M / properties-strip moved to "Deferred" in [design-sequencer.md](docs/mu-tant/design-sequencer.md) (rewritten to match). GatePatternTests rewritten for the new model. 28/28 mu-tant tests + 119/119 mu-clid tests pass; boundary PASS (136 mu-core files); mu-tant standalone smoke-tested (clean 4 s startup). Debug + Release clean at v1.0.673. | ✅ Fixed | 673 |

| 683 | **[Stage E — mu-tant `GatePattern` data model + per-voice storage + tests]** New [`mu_tant::GatePattern`](mu-tant/Source/Sequencer/GatePattern.h) — the data layer the drawable gate editor + audio-thread evaluator will both consume. `GatePattern` holds a flat `std::vector<GateEnvelope>` (cell + curveBend + options) plus a subdivision enum (Quarter / Eighth / Sixteenth / ThirtySecond). `GateEnvelope::value(phase01)` evaluates the envelope shape — linear decay at `curveBend=0`, concave (faster drop, audible gap) at negative bend, convex (sustains, late drop) at positive bend — via `pow(linearDecay, exponent)` with the bend mapped to `2^(-bend*2)`. `GateEnvelopeOptions` carries the design-spec gate-firing rules (reverse / probability / loopN/M / firstOnly / onStagedForChange). `PluginProcessor` gained `std::array<GatePattern, kMaxVoices> gatePatterns` (public, mutated under `voiceSlots[v].modLock`); the audio path doesn't yet apply the gate — that lands when `VoiceEngine` grows the gate stage between filter and insert. New [`GatePatternTests`](mu-tant/Source/Tests/GatePatternTests.cpp) covers: subdivision-to-cell-count math, linear decay endpoints, reverse polarity, concave/convex curve shaping, addOrReplaceEnvelope insert/replace/sort, removeEnvelopeAt no-op for absent cells, envelopeSpan to-next-envelope-or-pattern-end. | 666 | **[Audit fix]** MED — The full-preset load had two independent implementations (stopped = `applyPresetImmediate` tree→APVTS→`forceSync`; playing = `buildPreparedFullPreset`→`commitStagedFullPreset`) that could diverge by play-state. Unified onto a single prestage-then-commit path: `loadPreset` now always pre-builds the preset off the audio thread (`buildPreparedFullPreset`) and just triggers the switch — `stageFullPreset` (defer to loop point) when playing, `commitStagedFullPreset` (flip immediately) when stopped. The old `applyPresetImmediate` `.muclid` path is deleted, so stopped & playing loads are identical **by construction** (the divergence can't recur — no parity test needed) and a stopped load is now glitch-free with its sample disk I/O done off `rhythmsLock` (also tightens #663). | 663 | **[Audit fix]** HIGH — Preset-load + DAW host-state-restore raced the audio thread. `applyPresetImmediate` (stopped load) [PresetIO.cpp:1567](mu-clid/Source/Plugin/PresetIO.cpp#L1567) and `restoreStateFromTree` (host restore) [PresetIO.cpp:929](mu-clid/Source/Plugin/PresetIO.cpp#L929) rebuilt `voiceEngines[]` and swapped each `VoiceEngine` sample (`loadFile`/`clearSample`) with **no** serialisation; the prestaged `commitStagedFullPreset` had `suspendProcessing` but no `rhythmsLock` (which doesn't block an in-flight `processBlock`). Fixed by wrapping each mutation region in `suspendProcessing(true)` + `ScopedLock(rhythmsLock)` — the canonical mutator pattern (`loadSampleForRhythm`, `swapRhythms`). Deadlock-free: under `apvtsLoading`, `syncRhythmParam` only touches `r.voiceParams` under its own `voiceParamsLock`, and the audio thread bails via the tryLock while we hold `rhythmsLock`. Playing hot-swap stays glitch-free (lock only around the fast in-memory install, released before the APVTS finalize); stopped-load / project-reload hold the lock across sample disk I/O (brief silence if mid-playback — acceptable, non-real-time). `PresetIO.cpp` only. | 660 | **[Architecture — MIDI program-change path lifted from mu-clid into mu-core. New mu-family plugins (mu-tant, mu-toni) get the entire PC infrastructure for free.]** Pre-fix, mu-clid owned the FIFO + audio-thread scan + message-thread drain + the `MidiPresetMap` / `MidiFullPresetMap` storage classes + the `MidiPresetsPanel` / `MidiFullPresetsPanel` UI + the `PresetBrowser` overlay — even though every mu-family plugin will want the same channel-1-to-8 + channel-9 PC model. **Changes:** (1) [mu-core/Plugin/ProcessorBase.h](mu-core/Plugin/ProcessorBase.h) gained public `midiPresetMap` + `midiFullPresetMap` members, a private FIFO + queue, `scanMidiProgramChanges(midi)` (audio-thread) and `drainPendingMidiProgramChanges()` (message-thread), plus four pure-virtuals for the plugin-specific bits: `getPerSlotPresetDir/Extension()`, `getFullPresetDir/Extension()`, `applyMidiPresetSlot(int, juce::File)`, `applyFullMidiPreset(juce::File)`. ProcessorBase does NOT inherit AsyncUpdater — derived keeps full control of its async lifecycle (hot-swap etc.); the audio scan returns `bool needAsync` so derived can `triggerAsyncUpdate()` itself. (2) `MidiPresetMap` / `MidiFullPresetMap` lost their hard-coded `getDefaultFile()`; replaced with a `setStorageFile(juce::File)` that the consuming plugin calls once at startup before `load()`. File schema unchanged (existing user JSON keeps working). (3) `MidiPresetsPanel` / `MidiFullPresetsPanel` / `PresetBrowser` all moved to [mu-core/UI/](mu-core/UI/); panels now take `ProcessorBase&` and read file-extension + browser-root from the new virtuals. Browser uses `MuLookAndFeel` directly (no mu-clid alias). (4) `mu-clid::PluginProcessor`: the maps + FIFO + queue + audio-scan + drain were all deleted (now on base); the four virtuals are tiny overrides — `stageRhythmPreset`, `loadPreset`, `getRhythmsDir`, `getPresetsDir`, "muRhyth", "muclid". | 659 | **[Staging badge (#658) + demo banner backgrounds were invisible — `MuLookAndFeel::drawLabel` skipped `Label::backgroundColourId`]** Pre-fix the LookAndFeel override at [mu-core/UI/Components/MuLookAndFeel.cpp:264](mu-core/UI/Components/MuLookAndFeel.cpp#L264) only drew text — never filled the label background — so any Label using `backgroundColourId` for a coloured pill / banner appeared as bare text on the underlying component. | 653 | **[Full-preset hot-swap defers to the loop point — prestage + tail-out]** Loading a full `.muclid` preset while the sequencer is playing now stages the swap and commits it at the next loop point instead of applying instantly (matching per-rhythm hot-swap). **Prestage**: all voices/samples/rhythms are built off the audio thread at load time (`PresetIO::buildPreparedFullPreset` → `HotSwapStager::PreparedFullPreset`); the commit is just fast in-memory moves under one `suspendProcessing` (`commitStagedFullPreset`), so no disk I/O at the boundary. **Tail-out**: outgoing voices are retired (retire-then-swap, same machinery as the per-rhythm path) so they ring out their sample/amp-env tail across the boundary rather than hard-cutting; slots a smaller preset drops are cut. **Loop point**: waits for the master loop when one is defined (`mstrLoop>0`), else falls back to rhythm 0's loop — fixes a hang where a free-running swap waited for a master loop that never wraps. **UI**: new `onPresetSwapCommitted` callback refreshes rhythm tabs / sidebar / mixer after a deferred commit; cleared in the editor dtor (UAF guard). | 648 | **[Default rhythm RhythmCircle (main panel + sidebar mini) drew no hits on a fresh standalone open; audio played the pattern correctly]** Root cause: the audio thread only writes `lastEuclidOverrides[r]` inside the `runModulationPass` block, which is gated on `matrixHasAssignments || prevMatrixHadAssignments[r]` ([Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.cpp:458-462](Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.cpp#L458-L462)). For a rhythm with no modulation assignments — i.e. the default rhythm on startup — that branch never runs, so `lastEuclidOverrides[0]` stays at the C++ default `EuclidGenOverrides{}` (hits=0, rotate=0…). [Source/UI/RhythmPanel.cpp:499-500](Source/UI/RhythmPanel.cpp#L499-L500) (and [Source/UI/SidebarItem.cpp:81](Source/UI/SidebarItem.cpp#L81)) fetched the overrides via `proc.getModulatedEuclidOverrides(...)` and called `r.genA.getStepTypes(ov.a)`, which passes `ov.hits=0` into `EuclideanGenerator::generate` → empty pattern. The audio thread, meanwhile, plays the rhythm using `r.genA.hits=4` directly, so the audio was correct while the visual was blank. Loading a preset masked the bug because the preset's recently-active modulation pass had populated the overrides; resetting to default broke it again. **Fix**: [Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.h:276-303](Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.h#L276-L303) `getModulatedEuclidOverrides(int)` now returns the rhythm's base genA/B/C values when the modulation matrix has no assignments, falling back to `lastEuclidOverrides[r]` only when modulation is actually live. Added a `const Rhythm& getRhythm(int) const` overload to [Source/Sequencer/SequencerEngine.h:34](Source/Sequencer/SequencerEngine.h#L34) + [.cpp:83-87](Source/Sequencer/SequencerEngine.cpp#L83-L87) and forwarded it through [Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.h:134](Source/Plugin/PluginProcessor.h#L134) so the const `getModulatedEuclidOverrides` can read the rhythm without violating const-correctness on the SidebarItem's `const PluginProcessor*` handle. **Wider pattern**: any future "UI reads modulated state" path should similarly fall back to base values when modulation isn't running — `lastEuclidOverrides` is a *live-modulated* snapshot, not a *canonical view*. The comment in `getModulatedEuclidOverrides` documents the gotcha. **Regression test**: open standalone with a fresh state (no preset loaded) → confirm the default 16-step / 4-hit pattern shows 4 hits on the outer ring in both the main RhythmCircle and the SidebarItem mini-circle. Add a hit count change via knob → confirm ring updates immediately. Assign a Uni mod to euclid.a.hits → confirm #642's modulated-arc behaviour still works. 0 failures across 19 test classes.
